Section 3: File Contents
-----------------------
File: ./analyze_project.sh
----------------
     1	#!/bin/bash
     2	
     3	# Output file
     4	OUTPUT_FILE="project_analysis.txt"
     5	
     6	# Clear the output file if it exists
     7	> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
     8	
     9	# Add header with date
    10	echo "MERN Project Analysis" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    11	echo "Generated on: $(date)" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    12	echo "==================================" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    13	echo "" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    14	
    15	# Section 1: Directory Structure
    16	echo "Section 1: Directory Structure" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    17	echo "-----------------------------" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    18	# Exclude both node_modules and .git
    19	tree -I "node_modules|.git" --noreport . >> "$OUTPUT_FILE" 2>/dev/null || echo "Tree command failed (install with 'sudo apt install tree' or equivalent)" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    20	echo "" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    21	
    22	# Section 2: File Details
    23	echo "Section 2: File Details" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    24	echo "----------------------" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    25	# Exclude both node_modules and .git in find
    26	find . -type f -not -path "*/node_modules/*" -not -path "*/.git/*" | sort | while read -r file; do
    27	    echo "File: $file" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    28	    echo "Size: $(stat -c %s "$file") bytes" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    29	    echo "Permissions: $(stat -c %A "$file")" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    30	    echo "Last Modified: $(stat -c %y "$file")" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    31	    echo "" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    32	done
    33	
    34	# Section 3: File Contents
    35	echo "Section 3: File Contents" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    36	echo "-----------------------" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    37	find . -type f -not -path "*/node_modules/*" -not -path "*/.git/*" | sort | while read -r file; do
    38	    # Skip binary files and common non-code files
    39	    if [[ ! $file =~ \.(png|jpg|jpeg|gif|svg|ico|pdf|bin|zip|tar|gz)$ ]]; then
    40	        echo "File: $file" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    41	        echo "----------------" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    42	        # Add file content with line numbers, handle errors silently
    43	        cat -n "$file" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE" 2>/dev/null || echo "Unable to read file contents" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    44	        echo "" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    45	        echo "=================" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    46	        echo "" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    47	    else
    48	        echo "File: $file" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    49	        echo "----------------" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    50	        echo "(Binary file - contents not displayed)" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    51	        echo "=================" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    52	        echo "" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    53	    fi
    54	done
    55	
    56	# Section 4: Project Summary
    57	echo "Section 4: Project Summary" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    58	echo "-------------------------" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    59	echo "Total Directories: $(find . -type d -not -path '*/node_modules/*' -not -path '*/.git/*' | wc -l)" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    60	echo "Total Files: $(find . -type f -not -path '*/node_modules/*' -not -path '*/.git/*' | wc -l)" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    61	echo "Total Size: $(find . -type f -not -path '*/node_modules/*' -not -path '*/.git/*' -exec stat -c %s {} \; | awk '{sum += $1} END {print sum}') bytes" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    62	echo "" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    63	
    64	echo "Project analysis complete. Results saved in $OUTPUT_FILE"

File: ./backend/controllers/contactController.js
----------------
     1	const Contact = require('../models/Contact');
     2	const { parseCSV } = require('../utils/csvParser');
     3	const fs = require('fs');
     4	
     5	const uploadContacts = async (req, res) => {
     6	  if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No file uploaded' });
     7	
     8	  try {
     9	    const contacts = await parseCSV(req.file.path);
    10	    console.log(`Parsed ${contacts.length} contacts from CSV`);
    11	
    12	    // Check for existing phone numbers
    13	    const phoneNumbers = contacts.map(c => c.phone_number);
    14	    const existingContacts = await Contact.find({ phone_number: { $in: phoneNumbers } });
    15	    const existingPhoneNumbers = new Set(existingContacts.map(c => c.phone_number));
    16	
    17	    // Filter out duplicates
    18	    const newContacts = contacts.filter(c => !existingPhoneNumbers.has(c.phone_number));
    19	    const skippedCount = contacts.length - newContacts.length;
    20	
    21	    let insertedCount = 0;
    22	    if (newContacts.length > 0) {
    23	      const result = await Contact.insertMany(newContacts, { ordered: false });
    24	      insertedCount = result.length;
    25	    }
    26	
    27	    fs.unlinkSync(req.file.path); // Clean up
    28	
    29	    res.status(200).json({
    30	      message: 'Contacts processed successfully',
    31	      inserted: insertedCount,
    32	      skipped: skippedCount,
    33	    });
    34	  } catch (err) {
    35	    console.error('Error in uploadContacts:', err);
    36	    fs.unlinkSync(req.file.path); // Clean up
    37	    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message || 'Failed to process upload' });
    38	  }
    39	};
    40	
    41	const getContacts = async (req, res) => {
    42	  try {
    43	    const contacts = await Contact.find();
    44	    res.status(200).json(contacts);
    45	  } catch (err) {
    46	    console.error('Error in getContacts:', err);
    47	    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
    48	  }
    49	};
    50	
    51	module.exports = { uploadContacts, getContacts };

File: ./backend/controllers/messageController.js
----------------
     1	const Message = require('../models/Message');
     2	
     3	const createMessage = async (req, res) => {
     4	  const { contact_id, template_id } = req.body;
     5	  if (!contact_id || !template_id) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Contact ID and Template ID are required' });
     6	
     7	  try {
     8	    const message = new Message({ contact_id, template_id, mobile_id: 'unknown' }); // Default mobile_id
     9	    await message.save();
    10	    res.status(201).json(message);
    11	  } catch (err) {
    12	    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
    13	  }
    14	};
    15	
    16	const getMessages = async (req, res) => {
    17	  try {
    18	    const page = parseInt(req.query.page) || 1;
    19	    const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit) || 10;
    20	    const skip = (page - 1)*limit;
    21	    const { startDate, endDate, mobileId } = req.query;
    22	    const query = {};
    23	    if (startDate && endDate) {
    24	      query.datetime = { $gte: new Date(startDate), $lte: new Date(endDate) };
    25	    }
    26	    if (mobileId) {
    27	      query.mobile_id = mobileId;
    28	    }
    29	
    30	    const messages = await Message.find(query)
    31	    .skip(skip)
    32	    .limit(limit)
    33	    .populate('contact_id', 'name phone_number')
    34	    .populate('template_id', 'content')
    35	    .sort({ datetime: -1 });
    36	
    37	      const totalMessages = await Message.countDocuments();
    38	
    39	      res.status(200).json({
    40	        totalMessages,
    41	        totalPages: Math.ceil(totalMessages / limit),
    42	        currentPage: page,
    43	        messages,
    44	      });
    45	      
    46	  } catch (err) {
    47	    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
    48	  }
    49	};
    50	
    51	const getPendingMessages = async (req, res) => {
    52	  try {
    53	    const messages = await Message.find({ status: 'Pending' })
    54	      .populate('contact_id', 'phone_number')
    55	      .populate('template_id', 'content');
    56	    res.status(200).json(messages);
    57	  } catch (err) {
    58	    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
    59	  }
    60	};
    61	
    62	const updateMessageStatus = async (req, res) => {
    63	  const { status, mobile_id } = req.body;
    64	  try {
    65	    const message = await Message.findByIdAndUpdate(
    66	      req.params.id,
    67	      { status, mobile_id, datetime: new Date() },
    68	      { new: true }
    69	    ).populate('contact_id', 'phone_number').populate('template_id', 'content');
    70	    if (!message) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Message not found' });
    71	    res.status(200).json(message);
    72	  } catch (err) {
    73	    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
    74	  }
    75	};
    76	
    77	 const getAggregatedStats = async (req, res) => {
    78	  const { startDate, endDate } = req.query;
    79	  const match = startDate && endDate ? {
    80	    datetime: { $gte: new Date(startDate), $lte: new Date(endDate) }
    81	  } : {};
    82	  const stats = await Message.aggregate([
    83	    { $match: match },
    84	    {
    85	      $group: {
    86	        _id: null,
    87	        totalSent: { $sum: { $cond: [{ $eq: ['$status', 'Sent'] }, 1, 0] } },
    88	        totalFailed: { $sum: { $cond: [{ $eq: ['$status', 'Failed'] }, 1, 0] } },
    89	        totalPending: { $sum: { $cond: [{ $eq: ['$status', 'Pending'] }, 1, 0] } },
    90	      },
    91	    },
    92	  ]);
    93	  res.json(stats[0] || { totalSent: 0, totalFailed: 0, totalPending: 0 });
    94	};
    95	const getMobileStats = async (req, res) => {
    96	  const { startDate, endDate } = req.query;
    97	  const match = startDate && endDate ? {
    98	    datetime: { $gte: new Date(startDate), $lte: new Date(endDate) }
    99	  } : {};
   100	
   101	  const stats = await Message.aggregate([
   102	    { $match: match },
   103	    {
   104	      $group: {
   105	        _id: '$mobile_id',
   106	        sent: { $sum: { $cond: [{ $eq: ['$status', 'Sent'] }, 1, 0] } },
   107	        failed: { $sum: { $cond: [{ $eq: ['$status', 'Failed'] }, 1, 0] } },
   108	        pending: { $sum: { $cond: [{ $eq: ['$status', 'Pending'] }, 1, 0] } },
   109	      },
   110	    },
   111	  ]);
   112	  res.json(stats);
   113	};
   114	
   115	
   116	
   117	module.exports = { createMessage, getMessages, getPendingMessages, updateMessageStatus, getAggregatedStats, getMobileStats };

File: ./backend/middleware/auth.js
----------------
     1	const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
     2	
     3	module.exports = function(req, res, next) {
     4	  const token = req.header('x-auth-token');
     5	  // Check if no token
     6	  if (!token) {
     7	    return res.status(401).json({ msg: 'No token, authorization denied' });
     8	  }
     9	
    10	  // Verify token
    11	  try {
    12	    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET);
    13	    req.user = decoded.user;
    14	    next();
    15	  } catch (err) {
    16	    res.status(401).json({ msg: 'Token is not valid' });
    17	  }
    18	};

    39	    required: true
    40	  },
    41	  estimatedHours: {
    42	    type: Number,
    43	    min: 0
    44	  },
    45	  actualHours: {
    46	    type: Number,
    47	    min: 0,
    48	    default: 0
    49	  },
    50	  progress: {
    51	    type: Number,
    52	    min: 0,
    53	    max: 100,
    54	    default: 0
    55	  },
    56	  dependencies: [{
    57	    type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,
    58	    ref: 'Task'
    59	  }],
    60	  comments: [{
    61	    user: {
    62	      type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,
    63	      ref: 'User'
    64	    },
    65	    text: String,
    66	    createdAt: {
    67	      type: Date,
    68	      default: Date.now
    69	    }
    70	  }],
    71	  attachments: [{
    72	    filename: String,
    73	    path: String,
    74	    uploadedBy: {
    75	      type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,
    76	      ref: 'User'
    77	    },
    78	    uploadedAt: {
    79	      type: Date,
    80	      default: Date.now
    81	    }
    82	  }],
    83	  customFields: {
    84	    type: Map,
    85	    of: mongoose.Schema.Types.Mixed
    86	  }
    87	}, {
    88	  timestamps: true
    89	});
    90	
    91	// Indexes for better query performance
    92	taskSchema.index({ project: 1 });
    93	taskSchema.index({ assignedTo: 1 });
    94	taskSchema.index({ status: 1 });
    95	taskSchema.index({ deadline: 1 });
    96	
    97	const Task = mongoose.model('Task', taskSchema);
    98	
    99	module.exports = Task;

File: ./backend/models/User.js
----------------
     1	const mongoose = require('mongoose');
     2	const bcrypt = require('bcryptjs');
     3	
     4	const userSchema = new mongoose.Schema({
     5	  name: {
     6	    type: String,
     7	    required: true,
     8	    trim: true
     9	  },
    10	  phone: {
    11	    type: String,
    12	    required: true,
    13	    unique: true,
    14	    trim: true
    15	  },
    16	  email: {
    17	    type: String,
    18	    unique: true,
    19	    trim: true,
    20	    lowercase: true
    21	  },
    22	  password: {
    23	    type: String,
    24	    required: true,
    25	    minlength: 6
    26	  },
    27	  role: {
    28	    type: String,
    29	    enum: ['admin', 'manager', 'employee', 'client'],
    30	    default: 'employee'
    31	  },
    32	  department: {
    33	    type: String,
    34	    trim: true
    35	  },
    36	  isActive: {
    37	    type: Boolean,
    38	    default: true
    39	  },
    40	  lastLogin: {
    41	    type: Date
    42	  }
    43	}, {
    44	  timestamps: true
    45	});
    46	
    47	// Hash password before saving
    48	userSchema.pre('save', async function(next) {
    49	  if (this.isModified('password')) {
    50	    this.password = await bcrypt.hash(this.password, 8);
    51	  }
    52	  next();
    53	});
    54	
    55	// Method to compare password for login
    56	userSchema.methods.comparePassword = async function(candidatePassword) {
    57	  return bcrypt.compare(candidatePassword, this.password);
    58	};
    59	
    60	const User = mongoose.model('User', userSchema);
    61	
    62	module.exports = User;

File: ./backend/routes/auth.js
----------------
     1	const express = require('express');
     2	const router = express.Router();
     3	const bcrypt = require('bcryptjs');
     4	const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
     5	const { body, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
     6	const User = require('../models/User');
     7	
     8	// @route   POST api/auth/register
     9	// @desc    Register a user
    10	// @access  Public
    11	router.post('/register', [
    12	  body('name', 'Name is required').not().isEmpty(),
    13	  body('email', 'Please include a valid email').isEmail(),
    14	  body('password', 'Please enter a password with 6 or more characters').isLength({ min: 6 })
    15	], async (req, res) => {
    16	  const errors = validationResult(req);
    17	  if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
    18	    return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    19	  }
    20	
    21	  const { name, email, password, phone, role, department } = req.body;
    22	
    23	  try {
    24	    // Check if user exists
    25	    let user = await User.findOne({ email });
    26	    if (user) {
    27	      return res.status(400).json({ msg: 'User already exists' });
    28	    }
    29	
    30	    // Create new user
    31	    user = new User({
    32	      name,
    33	      email,
    34	      password,
    35	      phone,
    36	      role: role || 'employee',
    37	      department
    38	    });
    39	
    40	    await user.save();
    41	
    42	    // Create JWT token
    43	    const payload = {
    44	      user: {
    45	        id: user.id
    46	      }
    47	    };
    48	
    49	    jwt.sign(
    50	      payload,
    51	      process.env.JWT_SECRET,
    52	      { expiresIn: '24h' },
    53	      (err, token) => {
    54	        if (err) throw err;
    55	        res.json({ token });
    56	      }
    57	    );
    58	  } catch (err) {
    59	    console.error(err.message);
    60	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
    61	  }
    62	});
    63	
    64	// @route   POST api/auth/login
    65	// @desc    Authenticate user & get token
    66	// @access  Public
    67	router.post('/login', async (req, res) => {
    68	  const { email, password } = req.body;
    69	
    70	  try {
    71	    // Check if user exists
    72	    let user = await User.findOne({ email });
    73	    if (!user) {
    74	      return res.status(400).json({ msg: 'Invalid credentials' });
    75	    }
    76	    // Check password
    77	    const isMatch = await user.comparePassword(password);
    78	    if (!isMatch) {
    79	      return res.status(400).json({ msg: 'Invalid credentials' });
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    // Create JWT token
    83	    const payload = {
    84	      user: {
    85	        id: user._id
    86	      }
    87	    };
    88	
    89	    jwt.sign(
    90	      payload,
    91	      process.env.JWT_SECRET,
    92	      { expiresIn: '24h' },
    93	      (err, token) => {
    94	        if (err) throw err;
    95	        res.json({ token });
    96	      }
    97	    );
    98	  } catch (err) {
    99	    console.error(err.message);
   100	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
   101	  }
   102	});
   103	
   104	// @route   GET api/auth/verify
   105	// @desc    Verify token and get user data
   106	// @access  Private
   107	router.get('/verify', async (req, res) => {
   108	  try {
   109	    const token = req.header('x-auth-token');
   110	    if (!token) {
   111	      return res.status(401).json({ msg: 'No token, authorization denied' });
   112	    }
   113	
   114	    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET);
   115	    const user = await User.findById(decoded.user.id).select('-password');
   116	    res.json(user);
   117	  } catch (err) {
   118	    console.error(err.message);
   119	    res.status(401).json({ msg: 'Token is not valid' });
   120	  }
   121	});
   122	
   123	
   124	// @route   GET api/auth/users/:role
   125	// @desc    Get users with specific role
   126	// @access  Private
   127	router.get('/users/:role', async (req, res) => {
   128	  try {
   129	    const users = await User.find({ role: req.params.role }).select('name email department');
   130	    res.json(users);
   131	  } catch (err) {
   132	    console.error(err.message);
   133	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
   134	  }
   135	});
   136	
   137	module.exports = router;

File: ./backend/routes/deadlineExtensions.js
----------------
     1	const express = require('express');
     2	const router = express.Router();
     3	const { body, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
     4	const auth = require('../middleware/auth');
     5	const DeadlineExtension = require('../models/DeadlineExtension');
     6	const Task = require('../models/Task');
     7	const User = require('../models/User');
     8	const Project = require('../models/Project');
     9	
    10	// @route   GET api/deadline-extensions
    11	// @desc    Get all deadline extensions
    12	// @access  Private
    13	router.get('/', auth, async (req, res) => {
    14	  try {
    15	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
    16	    let extensions;
    17	
    18	    if (user.role === 'admin') {
    19	      extensions = await DeadlineExtension.find()
    20	        .populate('task', 'name project')
    21	        .populate('requestedBy', 'name email')
    22	        .populate('approvedBy', 'name email');
    23	    } else if (user.role === 'manager') {
    24	      const tasks = await Task.find({ project: { $in: await getManagedProjects(req.user.id) } });
    25	      const taskIds = tasks.map(t => t._id);
    26	      extensions = await DeadlineExtension.find({ task: { $in: taskIds } })
    27	        .populate('task', 'name project')
    28	        .populate('requestedBy', 'name email')
    29	        .populate('approvedBy', 'name email');
    30	    } else {
    31	      extensions = await DeadlineExtension.find({ requestedBy: req.user.id })
    32	        .populate('task', 'name project')
    33	        .populate('requestedBy', 'name email')
    34	        .populate('approvedBy', 'name email');
    35	    }
    36	
    37	    res.json(extensions);
    38	  } catch (err) {
    39	    console.error(err.message);
    40	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
    41	  }
    42	});
    43	
    44	// @route   POST api/deadline-extensions
    45	// @desc    Request a deadline extension
    46	// @access  Private
    47	router.post('/', auth,
    48	  async (req, res) => {
    49	    const {
    50	      projectId,
    51	      newDeadline,
    52	      reason,
    53	      category
    54	    } = req.body;
    55	  try {
    56	    const newDeadlineDate = new Date(newDeadline);
    57	    if (isNaN(newDeadlineDate.getTime())) {
    58	      return res.status(400).json({ msg: 'Invalid newDeadline date' });
    59	    }
    60	
    61	    const project = await Project.findById(req.body.projectId);
    62	    if (!project) {
    63	      return res.status(404).json({ msg: 'Project not found' });
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    // Check if user is admin
    67	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
    68	    if (user.role !== 'admin') {
    69	      return res.status(403).json({ msg: 'Not authorized to request extension for this task' });
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    const newExtension = new DeadlineExtension({
    73	      project: projectId,
    74	      requestedBy: req.user.id,
    75	      oldDeadline: project.endDate,
    76	       newDeadline: newDeadlineDate,
    77	      reason,
    78	      category
    79	    });
    80	    project.endDate = newDeadlineDate;
    81	    await Promise.all([newExtension.save(), project.save()]);
    82	
    83	    res.status(200).json({
    84	      extension: newExtension,
    85	      project: {
    86	        _id: project._id,
    87	        endDate: project.endDate,
    88	      },
    89	    });
    90	  } catch (err) {
    91	    console.error(err.message);
    92	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
    93	  }
    94	});
    95	
    96	//get the deadline by project id
    97	router.get('/:projectId',auth, async(req, res)=>{
    98	    try{
    99	      const projectId = req.params.projectId;
   100	      const extesntions = await DeadlineExtension.find({project: projectId});
   101	      res.status(200).json(extesntions);
   102	    }catch(error){
   103	      console.log(error.message)
   104	      res.status(500).send('Server error');
   105	    }
   106	})
   107	
   108	// Helper function to get projects managed by a user
   109	async function getManagedProjects(userId) {
   110	  const projects = await Project.find({ manager: userId });
   111	  return projects.map(p => p._id);
   112	}
   113	
   114	module.exports = router;

File: ./backend/routes/leadRoutes.js

     1	const route = require('express').Router();
     2	const Lead = require('../models/Lead');
     3	const User = require('../models/User');
     4	
     5	//Create a new lead
     6	route.post('/', async(req, res) =>{
     7	    const {title, remark, requestedData} = req.body;
     8	    //Validation
     9	    if(!title || !remark || !requestedData){
    10	        return res.status(400).json({message: 'All fields are required'});
    11	    }
    12	    let requestedDataObj = {
    13	        title: requestedData,
    14	    }
    15	    try{
    16	        const client = await User.findOne({role: 'client'});
    17	        if(!client){
    18	            return res.status(404).json({message: 'Client not found'});
    19	        }
    20	        const lead = new Lead({
    21	            title,
    22	            client: client._id,
    23	            remark,
    24	            requestedData:requestedDataObj,
    25	        });
    26	        await lead.save();
    27	        res.status(201).json({message: 'Lead created successfully', lead});
    28	    }catch(err){
    29	        console.error(err);
    30	        res.status(500).json({message: 'Server error'});
    31	    }
    32	}
    33	)
    34	
    35	//Get all leads
    36	route.get('/', async(req, res) =>{
    37	    try{
    38	        const leads = await Lead.find().populate('client', 'name phone');
    39	        res.status(200).json(leads);
    40	    }catch(err){
    41	        console.error(err);
    42	        res.status(500).json({message: 'Server error'});
    43	    }
    44	})
    45	//delete a lead
    46	route.delete('/:id', async(req, res) =>{
    47	    try{
    48	        const lead = await Lead.findByIdAndDelete(req.params.id);
    49	        if(!lead){
    50	            return res.status(404).json({message: 'Lead not found'});
    51	        }
    52	        res.status(200).json({message: 'Lead deleted successfully'});
    53	    }catch(err){
    54	        console.error(err);
    55	        res.status(500).json({message: 'Server error'})
    56	    }
    57	})
    58

File: ./backend/routes/pendencies.js

     1	const express = require('express');
     2	const router = express.Router();
     3	const { body, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
     4	const auth = require('../middleware/auth');
     5	const Pendency = require('../models/Pendency');
     6	const Task = require('../models/Task');
     7	const User = require('../models/User');
     8	const Project = require('../models/Project');
     9	
    10	// @route   GET api/pendencies
    11	// @desc    Get all pendencies
    12	// @access  Private
    13	router.get('/', auth, async (req, res) => {
    14	  try {
    15	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
    16	    let pendencies;
    17	
    18	    if (user.role === 'admin') {
    19	      pendencies = await Pendency.find()
    20	        .populate('task', 'name project')
    21	        .populate('reportedBy', 'name email');
    22	    } else if (user.role === 'manager') {
    23	      const tasks = await Task.find({ project: { $in: await getManagedProjects(req.user.id) } });
    24	      const taskIds = tasks.map(t => t._id);
    25	      pendencies = await Pendency.find({ task: { $in: taskIds } })
    26	        .populate('task', 'name project')
    27	        .populate('reportedBy', 'name email');
    28	    } else {
    29	      pendencies = await Pendency.find({ reportedBy: req.user.id })
    30	        .populate('task', 'name project')
    31	        .populate('reportedBy', 'name email');
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    res.json(pendencies);
    35	  } catch (err) {
    36	    console.error(err.message);
    37	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
    38	  }
    39	});
    40	
    41	// @route   POST api/pendencies
    42	// @desc    Report a pendency
    43	// @access  Private
    44	router.post('/', [
    45	  auth,
    46	  [
    47	    body('task', 'Task ID is required').not().isEmpty(),
    48	    body('category', 'Category is required').not().isEmpty(),
    49	    body('reason', 'Reason is required').not().isEmpty(),
    50	    body('subCategory', 'Sub-category is required').not().isEmpty()
    51	  ]
    52	], async (req, res) => {
    53	  const errors = validationResult(req);
    54	  if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
    55	    return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    56	  }
    57	
    58	  try {
    59	    const task = await Task.findById(req.body.task);
    60	    if (!task) {
    61	      return res.status(404).json({ msg: 'Task not found' });
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    // Check if user is assigned to the task
    65	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
    66	    if (user.role !== 'admin' && !task.assignedTo.includes(req.user.id)) {
    67	      return res.status(403).json({ msg: 'Not authorized to report pendency for this task' });
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    const {
    71	      task: taskId,
    72	      category,
    73	      reason,
    74	      subCategory,
    75	      expectedResolutionDate,
    76	      impact,
    77	      attachments
    78	    } = req.body;
    79	
    80	    const newPendency = new Pendency({
    81	      task: taskId,
    82	      reportedBy: req.user.id,
    83	      category,
    84	      reason,
    85	      subCategory,
    86	      expectedResolutionDate,
    87	      impact,
    88	      attachments
    89	    });
    90	
    91	    const pendency = await newPendency.save();
    92	    res.json(pendency);
    93	  } catch (err) {
    94	    console.error(err.message);
    95	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
    96	  }
    97	});
    98	
    99	// @route   PUT api/pendencies/:id/resolve
   100	// @desc    Resolve a pendency
   101	// @access  Private
   102	router.put('/:id/resolve', [
   103	  auth,
   104	  body('resolutionNotes', 'Resolution notes are required').not().isEmpty()
   105	], async (req, res) => {
   106	  const errors = validationResult(req);
   107	  if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
   108	    return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
   109	  }
   110	
   111	  try {
   112	    const pendency = await Pendency.findById(req.params.id);
   113	    if (!pendency) {
   114	      return res.status(404).json({ msg: 'Pendency not found' });
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
   118	    const task = await Task.findById(pendency.task);
   119	    const project = await Project.findById(task.project);
   120	
   121	    // Check authorization
   122	    if (user.role !== 'admin' && 
   123	        project.manager.toString() !== req.user.id && 
   124	        pendency.reportedBy.toString() !== req.user.id) {
   125	      return res.status(403).json({ msg: 'Not authorized to resolve this pendency' });
   126	    }
   127	
   128	    pendency.status = 'resolved';
   129	    pendency.actualResolutionDate = Date.now();
   130	    pendency.resolutionNotes = req.body.resolutionNotes;
   131	    await pendency.save();
   132	
   133	    res.json(pendency);
   134	  } catch (err) {
   135	    console.error(err.message);
   136	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
   137	  }
   138	});
   139	
   140	// @route   POST api/pendencies/:id/comments
   141	// @desc    Add a comment to a pendency
   142	// @access  Private
   143	router.post('/:id/comments', [
   144	  auth,
   145	  body('text', 'Comment text is required').not().isEmpty()
   146	], async (req, res) => {
   147	  const errors = validationResult(req);
   148	  if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
   149	    return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
   150	  }
   151	
   152	  try {
   153	    const pendency = await Pendency.findById(req.params.id);
   154	    if (!pendency) {
   155	      return res.status(404).json({ msg: 'Pendency not found' });
   156	    }
   157	
   158	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
   159	    const task = await Task.findById(pendency.task);
   160	    const project = await Project.findById(task.project);
   161	
   162	    // Check authorization
   163	    if (user.role !== 'admin' && 
   164	        project.manager.toString() !== req.user.id && 
   165	        pendency.reportedBy.toString() !== req.user.id) {
   166	      return res.status(403).json({ msg: 'Not authorized to comment on this pendency' });
   167	    }
   168	
   169	    const newComment = {
   170	      user: req.user.id,
   171	      text: req.body.text
   172	    };
   173	
   174	    pendency.comments.unshift(newComment);
   175	    await pendency.save();
   176	    res.json(pendency.comments);
   177	  } catch (err) {
   178	    console.error(err.message);
   179	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
   180	  }
   181	});

     1	const express = require('express');
     2	const router = express.Router();
     3	const { body, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
     4	const auth = require('../middleware/auth');
     5	const Project = require('../models/Project');
     6	const User = require('../models/User');
     7	
     8	// @route   GET api/projects
     9	// @desc    Get all projects
    10	// @access  Private
    11	router.get('/', auth, async (req, res) => {
    12	  try {
    13	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
    14	    let projects;
    15	
    16	    if (user.role === 'admin') {
    17	      projects = await Project.find()
    18	        .populate({
    19	          path: 'team',
    20	          populate: [
    21	            { path: 'teamLeader', select: 'name' },
    22	            { path: 'teamMembers', select: 'name' }
    23	          ]
    24	        })
    25	        .populate('client', 'name');
    26	    } else if (user.role === 'manager') {
    27	      projects = await Project.find({ "team.teamLeader": req.user.id })
    28	        .populate('manager', 'name email')
    29	        .populate('teamMembers', 'name email');
    30	    } else {
    31	      projects = await Project.find({ 'team.teamMember': req.user.id })
    32	        .populate('manager', 'name email')
    33	        .populate('teamMembers', 'name email');
    34	    }
    35	
    36	    res.json(projects);
    37	  } catch (err) {
    38	    console.error(err.message);
    39	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
    40	  }
    41	});
    42	
    43	// @route   POST api/projects
    44	// @desc    Create a project
    45	// @access  Private (Admin/Manager)
    46	router.post('/', auth, async (req, res) => {
    47	  try {
    48	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
    49	    if (user.role !== 'admin' && user.role !== 'manager') {
    50	      return res.status(403).json({ msg: 'Not authorized to create projects' });
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    const {
    54	      name,
    55	      description,
    56	      startDate,
    57	      endDate,
    58	      team,
    59	      client,
    60	      priority,
    61	      tags,
    62	    } = req.body;
    63	
    64	    const newProject = new Project({
    65	      name,
    66	      description,
    67	      startDate,
    68	      endDate,
    69	      team,
    70	      client,
    71	      priority,
    72	      tags,
    73	      createdBy: req.user.id
    74	    });
    75	    const project = await newProject.save();
    76	    res.json(project);
    77	  } catch (err) {
    78	    console.error(err.message);
    79	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
    80	  }
    81	});
    82	
    83	// @route   PUT api/projects/:id
    84	// @desc    Update a project
    85	// @access  Private (Admin/Manager)
    86	router.put('/:id', auth, async (req, res) => {
    87	  try {
    88	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
    89	    if (user.role !== 'admin' && user.role !== 'manager') {
    90	      return res.status(403).json({ msg: 'Not authorized to update projects' });
    91	    }
    92	
    93	    const project = await Project.findById(req.params.id);
    94	    if (!project) {
    95	      return res.status(404).json({ msg: 'Project not found' });
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    // Check if user is the manager of the project
    99	    if (user.role === 'manager' && project.manager.toString() !== req.user.id) {
   100	      return res.status(403).json({ msg: 'Not authorized to update this project' });
   101	    }
   102	
   103	    const {
   104	      name,
   105	      description,
   106	      status,
   107	      startDate,
   108	      endDate,
   109	      progress,
   110	      teamMembers,
   111	      client,
   112	      budget,
   113	      priority,
   114	      customFields,
   115	      tags
   116	    } = req.body;
   117	
   118	    // Update project fields
   119	    if (name) project.name = name;
   120	    if (description) project.description = description;
   121	    if (status) project.status = status;
   122	    if (startDate) project.startDate = startDate;
   123	    if (endDate) project.endDate = endDate;
   124	    if (progress) project.progress = progress;
   125	    if (teamMembers) project.teamMembers = teamMembers;
   126	    if (client) project.client = client;
   127	    if (budget) project.budget = budget;
   128	    if (priority) project.priority = priority;
   129	    if (customFields) project.customFields = customFields;
   130	    if (tags) project.tags = tags;
   131	
   132	    await project.save();
   133	    res.json(project);
   134	  } catch (err) {
   135	    console.error(err.message);
   136	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
   137	  }
   138	});
   139

File: ./backend/routes/tasks.js

     1	const express = require('express');
     2	const router = express.Router();
     3	const { body, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
     4	const auth = require('../middleware/auth');
     5	const Task = require('../models/Task');
     6	const Project = require('../models/Project');
     7	const User = require('../models/User');
     8	
     9	// @route   GET api/tasks
    10	// @desc    Get all tasks
    11	// @access  Private
    12	router.get('/', auth, async (req, res) => {
    13	  try {
    14	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
    15	    let tasks;
    16	
    17	    if (user.role === 'admin') {
    18	      tasks = await Task.find()
    19	        .populate('project', 'name')
    20	        .populate('assignedTo', 'name email')
    21	        .populate('dependencies', 'name');
    22	    } else if (user.role === 'manager') {
    23	      const projects = await Project.find({ manager: req.user.id });
    24	      const projectIds = projects.map(p => p._id);
    25	      tasks = await Task.find({ project: { $in: projectIds } })
    26	        .populate('project', 'name')
    27	        .populate('assignedTo', 'name email')
    28	        .populate('dependencies', 'name');
    29	    } else {
    30	      tasks = await Task.find({ assignedTo: req.user.id })
    31	        .populate('project', 'name')
    32	        .populate('assignedTo', 'name email')
    33	        .populate('dependencies', 'name');
    34	    }
    35	
    36	    res.json(tasks);
    37	  } catch (err) {
    38	    console.error(err.message);
    39	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
    40	  }
    41	});
    42	
    43	// @route   POST api/tasks
    44	// @desc    Create a task
    45	// @access  Private (Admin/Manager)
    46	router.post('/', [
    47	  auth,
    48	  [
    49	    body('name', 'Name is required').not().isEmpty(),
    50	    body('description', 'Description is required').not().isEmpty(),
    51	    body('project', 'Project is required').not().isEmpty(),
    52	    body('startDate', 'Start date is required').not().isEmpty(),
    53	    body('deadline', 'Deadline is required').not().isEmpty()
    54	  ]
    55	], async (req, res) => {
    56	  const errors = validationResult(req);
    57	  if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
    58	    return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    59	  }
    60	
    61	  try {
    62	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
    63	    if (user.role !== 'admin' && user.role !== 'manager') {
    64	      return res.status(403).json({ msg: 'Not authorized to create tasks' });
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    const project = await Project.findById(req.body.project);
    68	    if (!project) {
    69	      return res.status(404).json({ msg: 'Project not found' });
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    // Check if user is the manager of the project
    73	    if (user.role === 'manager' && project.manager.toString() !== req.user.id) {
    74	      return res.status(403).json({ msg: 'Not authorized to create tasks for this project' });
    75	    }
    76	
    77	    const {
    78	      name,
    79	      description,
    80	      project: projectId,
    81	      assignedTo,
    82	      priority,
    83	      startDate,
    84	      deadline,
    85	      estimatedHours,
    86	      dependencies,
    87	      customFields
    88	    } = req.body;
    89	
    90	    const newTask = new Task({
    91	      name,
    92	      description,
    93	      project: projectId,
    94	      assignedTo: assignedTo || [],
    95	      priority,
    96	      startDate,
    97	      deadline,
    98	      estimatedHours,
    99	      dependencies: dependencies || [],
   100	      customFields
   101	    });
   102	
   103	    const task = await newTask.save();
   104	    res.json(task);
   105	  } catch (err) {
   106	    console.error(err.message);
   107	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
   108	  }
   109	});
   110	
   111	// @route   PUT api/tasks/:id
   112	// @desc    Update a task
   113	// @access  Private
   114	router.put('/:id', auth, async (req, res) => {
   115	  try {
   116	    const task = await Task.findById(req.params.id);
   117	    if (!task) {
   118	      return res.status(404).json({ msg: 'Task not found' });
   119	    }
   120	
   121	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
   122	    const project = await Project.findById(task.project);
   123	
   124	    // Check authorization
   125	    if (user.role !== 'admin' && 
   126	        project.manager.toString() !== req.user.id && 
   127	        !task.assignedTo.includes(req.user.id)) {
   128	      return res.status(403).json({ msg: 'Not authorized to update this task' });
   129	    }
   130	
   131	    const {
   132	      name,
   133	      description,
   134	      status,
   135	      priority,
   136	      startDate,
   137	      deadline,
   138	      estimatedHours,
   139	      actualHours,
   140	      progress,
   141	      assignedTo,
   142	      dependencies,
   143	      customFields
   144	    } = req.body;
   145	
   146	    // Update task fields
   147	    if (name) task.name = name;
   148	    if (description) task.description = description;
   149	    if (status) task.status = status;
   150	    if (priority) task.priority = priority;
   151	    if (startDate) task.startDate = startDate;
   152	    if (deadline) task.deadline = deadline;
   153	    if (estimatedHours) task.estimatedHours = estimatedHours;
   154	    if (actualHours) task.actualHours = actualHours;
   155	    if (progress) task.progress = progress;
   156	    if (assignedTo) task.assignedTo = assignedTo;
   157	    if (dependencies) task.dependencies = dependencies;
   158	    if (customFields) task.customFields = customFields;
   159	
   160	    await task.save();
   161	    res.json(task);
   162	  } catch (err) {
   163	    console.error(err.message);
   164	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
   165	  }
   166	});
   167	
   168	// @route   DELETE api/tasks/:id
   169	// @desc    Delete a task
   170	// @access  Private (Admin/Manager)
   171	router.delete('/:id', auth, async (req, res) => {
   172	  try {
   173	    const task = await Task.findById(req.params.id);
   174	    if (!task) {
   175	      return res.status(404).json({ msg: 'Task not found' });
   176	    }
   177	
   178	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
   179	    const project = await Project.findById(task.project);
   180	
   181	    if (user.role !== 'admin' && project.manager.toString() !== req.user.id) {
   182	      return res.status(403).json({ msg: 'Not authorized to delete this task' });
   183	    }
   184	
   185	    await task.remove();
   186	    res.json({ msg: 'Task removed' });
   187	  } catch (err) {
   188	    console.error(err.message);
   189	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
   190	  }
   191	});
   192	
   193	// @route   GET api/tasks/:id
   194	// @desc    Get task by ID
   195	// @access  Private
   196	router.get('/:id', auth, async (req, res) => {
   197	  try {
   198	    const task = await Task.findById(req.params.id)
   199	      .populate('project', 'name')
   200	      .populate('assignedTo', 'name email')
   201	      .populate('dependencies', 'name');
   202	
   203	    if (!task) {
   204	      return res.status(404).json({ msg: 'Task not found' });
   205	    }
   206	
   207	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
   208	    const project = await Project.findById(task.project);
   209	
   210	    // Check authorization
   211	    if (user.role !== 'admin' && 
   212	        project.manager.toString() !== req.user.id && 
   213	        !task.assignedTo.includes(req.user.id)) {
   214	      return res.status(403).json({ msg: 'Not authorized to view this task' });
   215	    }
   216	
   217	    res.json(task);
   218	  } catch (err) {
   219	    console.error(err.message);
   220	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
   221	  }
   222	});
   223	
   224	// @route   POST api/tasks/:id/comments
   225	// @desc    Add a comment to a task
   226	// @access  Private
   227	router.post('/:id/comments', [
   228	  auth,
   229	  body('text', 'Comment text is required').not().isEmpty()
   230	], async (req, res) => {
   231	  const errors = validationResult(req);
   232	  if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
   233	    return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
   234	  }
   235	
   236	  try {
   237	    const task = await Task.findById(req.params.id);
   238	    if (!task) {
   239	      return res.status(404).json({ msg: 'Task not found' });
   240	    }
   241	
   242	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
   243	    const project = await Project.findById(task.project);
   244	
   245	    // Check authorization
   246	    if (user.role !== 'admin' && 
   247	        project.manager.toString() !== req.user.id && 
   248	        !task.assignedTo.includes(req.user.id)) {
   249	      return res.status(403).json({ msg: 'Not authorized to comment on this task' });
   250	    }
   251	
   252	    const newComment = {
   253	      user: req.user.id,
   254	      text: req.body.text
   255	    };
   256	
   257	    task.comments.unshift(newComment);
   258	    await task.save();
   259	    res.json(task.comments);
   260	  } catch (err) {
   261	    console.error(err.message);
   262	    res.status(500).send('Server error');
   263	  }
   264	});
   265	
   266	module.exports = router;

     1	require('dotenv').config();

     9	const app = express();

    11	// Middleware
    12	app.use(cors());
    13	app.use(express.json());
    14	app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));
    15	
    16	// MongoDB Connection
    17	mongoose.connect(process.env.MONGO_URI || 'mongodb+srv://rdmodels:YFpB8St0asdssde@dssdds.s7wamg6.mongodb.net/', {})

    22	app.use('/api/auth', require('./routes/auth'));
    23	app.use('/api/users', require('./routes/userRoutes'));
    24	app.use('/api/messages', require('./routes/messageRoutes'));
    25	app.use('/api/contacts', require('./routes/contactRoutes'));
    26	app.use('/api/templates', require('./routes/templateRoutes'));

    32	app.use('/api/teams', require('./routes/teamRoutes'))
    33	
    34	// Error handling middleware

    36	  console.error(err.stack);
    37	  res.status(500).json({
    38	    success: false,
    39	    message: 'Something went wrong!',
    40	    error: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? err.message : undefined
    41	  });
    42	});
    43	
    44	// 404 handler
    45	app.use((req, res) => {
    46	  res.status(404).json({
    47	    success: false,
    48	    message: 'Route not found'
    49	  });
    50	});
    51	
    52	const PORT = process.env.PORT || 5000;
    53	app.listen(PORT, () => {
    54	  console.log(`Server is running on port ${PORT}`);
    55	});

File: ./backend/utils/csvParser.js
----------------
     1	const fs = require('fs');
     2	const { parse } = require('csv-parse');
     3	
     4	const parseCSV = (filePath) => {
     5	  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
     6	    const results = [];
     7	    fs.createReadStream(filePath)
     8	      .pipe(parse({ columns: true, trim: true }))
     9	      .on('data', (row) => {
    10	        const contact = {
    11	          name: row.name,
    12	          phone_number: row.phone_number,
    13	          email: row.email || '',
    14	          whatsapp_number: row.whatsapp_number || '',
    15	          address: row.address || '',
    16	          additional_info: {},
    17	        };
    18	        // Capture any extra fields dynamically
    19	        for (const key in row) {
    20	          if (!['name', 'phone_number', 'email', 'whatsapp_number', 'address'].includes(key)) {
    21	            contact.additional_info[key] = row[key];
    22	          }
    23	        }
    24	        results.push(contact);
    25	      })
    26	      .on('end', () => resolve(results))
    27	      .on('error', (err) => reject(err));
    28	  });
    29	};
    30	
    31	module.exports = { parseCSV };

     1	# React + Vite
     2	
     3	This template provides a minimal setup to get React working in Vite with HMR and some ESLint rules.
     4	
     5	Currently, two official plugins are available:
     6	
     7	- [@vitejs/plugin-react](https://github.com/vitejs/vite-plugin-react/blob/main/packages/plugin-react/README.md) uses [Babel](https://babeljs.io/) for Fast Refresh
     8	- [@vitejs/plugin-react-swc](https://github.com/vitejs/vite-plugin-react-swc) uses [SWC](https://swc.rs/) for Fast Refresh
     9	
    10	## Expanding the ESLint configuration
    11	
    12	If you are developing a production application, we recommend using TypeScript and enable type-aware lint rules. Check out the [TS template](https://github.com/vitejs/vite/tree/main/packages/create-vite/template-react-ts) to integrate TypeScript and [`typescript-eslint`](https://typescript-eslint.io) in your project.

     4	export const uploadContacts = (file) => {
     5	  const formData = new FormData();
     6	  formData.append('file', file);
     7	  return axios.post(`${API_URL}/contacts/upload`, formData);

File: ./frontend/src/components/AddProjectOverlay.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
     2	
     3	function AddProjectOverlay({ isOpen, onClose, onAddProject, teams, clients }) {
     4	  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
     5	    name: '',
     6	    description: '',
     7	    startDate: '',
     8	    endDate: '',
     9	    team: '',
    10	    client: '',
    11	    priority: 'medium',
    12	    tags: []
    13	  });
    14	  
    15	  const [tagInput, setTagInput] = useState('');
    16	
    17	  useEffect(() => {
    18	    // Set default dates when the overlay opens
    19	    if (isOpen) {
    20	      const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
    21	      const nextYear = new Date();
    22	      nextYear.setFullYear(nextYear.getFullYear() + 1);
    23	      
    24	      setFormData(prev => ({
    25	        ...prev,
    26	        startDate: today,
    27	        endDate: nextYear.toISOString().split('T')[0]
    28	      }));
    29	    }
    30	  }, [isOpen]);
    31	
    32	  const handleChange = (e) => {
    33	    const { name, value } = e.target;
    34	    setFormData(prev => ({
    35	      ...prev,
    36	      [name]: value
    37	    }));
    38	  };
    39	
    40	  const handleAddTag = () => {
    41	    if (tagInput.trim() && !formData.tags.includes(tagInput.trim())) {
    42	      setFormData(prev => ({
    43	        ...prev,
    44	        tags: [...prev.tags, tagInput.trim()]
    45	      }));
    46	      setTagInput('');
    47	    }
    48	  };
    49	
    50	  const handleRemoveTag = (tagToRemove) => {
    51	    setFormData(prev => ({
    52	      ...prev,
    53	      tags: prev.tags.filter(tag => tag !== tagToRemove)
    54	    }));
    55	  };
    56	
    57	  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    58	    e.preventDefault();
    59	    if (!formData.name.trim()) return;
    60	    
    61	    // Format dates for API
    62	    const projectData = {
    63	      ...formData,
    64	      startDate: new Date(formData.startDate).toISOString(),
    65	      endDate: new Date(formData.endDate).toISOString()
    66	    };
    67	    
    68	    onAddProject(projectData);
    69	    
    70	    // Reset form
    71	    setFormData({
    72	      name: '',
    73	      description: '',
    74	      startDate: '',
    75	      endDate: '',
    76	      team: '',
    77	      client: '',
    78	      priority: 'medium',
    79	      tags: []
    80	    });
    81	    setTagInput('');
    82	    onClose();
    83	  };
    84	
    85	  if (!isOpen) return null;
    86	
    87	  return (
    88	    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 flex items-center justify-center z-50">
    89	      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 w-full max-w-2xl max-h-[90vh] overflow-y-auto">
    90	        <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-4">
    91	          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold">Add New Project</h2>
    92	          <button 
    93	            onClick={onClose}
    94	            className="text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-700"
    95	          >
    96	            <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" className="h-6 w-6" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor">
    97	              <path strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" strokeWidth={2} d="M6 18L18 6M6 6l12 12" />
    98	            </svg>
    99	          </button>
   100	        </div>
   101	        
   102	        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
   103	          {/* Project Name */}
   104	          <div className="md:col-span-2">
   105	            <label htmlFor="name" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
   106	              Project Name*
   107	            </label>
   108	            <input
   109	              type="text"
   110	              id="name"
   111	              name="name"
   112	              value={formData.name}
   113	              onChange={handleChange}
   114	              className="w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
   115	              required
   116	            />
   117	          </div>
   118	          
   119	          {/* Description */}
   120	          <div className="md:col-span-2">
   121	            <label htmlFor="description" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
   122	              Description
   123	            </label>
   124	            <textarea
   125	              id="description"
   126	              name="description"
   127	              value={formData.description}
   128	              onChange={handleChange}
   129	              className="w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
   130	              rows="3"
   131	            />
   132	          </div>
   133	          
   134	          {/* Start Date */}
   135	          <div>
   136	            <label htmlFor="startDate" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
   137	              Start Date*
   138	            </label>
   139	            <input
   140	              type="date"
   141	              id="startDate"
   142	              name="startDate"
   143	              value={formData.startDate}
   144	              onChange={handleChange}
   145	              className="w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
   146	              required
   147	            />
   148	          </div>
   149	          
   150	          {/* End Date */}
   151	          <div>
   152	            <label htmlFor="endDate" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
   153	              End Date*
   154	            </label>
   155	            <input
   156	              type="date"
   157	              id="endDate"
   158	              name="endDate"
   159	              value={formData.endDate}
   160	              onChange={handleChange}
   161	              className="w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
   162	              required
   163	            />
   164	          </div>
   165	          
   166	          {/* Team */}
   167	          <div>
   168	            <label htmlFor="team" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
   169	              Team*
   170	            </label>
   171	            <select
   172	              id="team"
   173	              name="team"
   174	              value={formData.team}
   175	              onChange={handleChange}
   176	              className="w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
   177	              required
   178	            >
   179	              <option value="">Select a team</option>
   180	              {teams?.map(team => (
   181	                <option key={team._id} value={team._id}>
   182	                  {team.name}
   183	                </option>
   184	              ))}
   185	            </select>
   186	          </div>
   187	          
   188	          {/* Client */}
   189	          <div>
   190	            <label htmlFor="client" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
   191	              Client*
   192	            </label>
   193	            <select
   194	              id="client"
   195	              name="client"
   196	              value={formData.client}
   197	              onChange={handleChange}
   198	              className="w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
   199	              required
   200	            >
   201	              <option value="">Select a client</option>
   202	              {clients?.map(client => (
   203	                <option key={client._id} value={client._id}>
   204	                  {client.name}
   205	                </option>
   206	              ))}
   207	            </select>
   208	          </div>
   209	          
   210	          {/* Priority */}
   211	          <div>
   212	            <label htmlFor="priority" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
   213	              Priority
   214	            </label>
   215	            <select
   216	              id="priority"
   217	              name="priority"
   218	              value={formData.priority}
   219	              onChange={handleChange}
   220	              className="w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
   221	            >
   222	              <option value="low">Low</option>
   223	              <option value="medium">Medium</option>
   224	              <option value="high">High</option>
   225	            </select>
   226	          </div>
   227	          
   228	          {/* Tags */}
   229	          <div className="md:col-span-2">
   230	            <label htmlFor="tags" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
   231	              Tags
   232	            </label>
   233	            <div className="flex items-center">
   234	              <input
   235	                type="text"
   236	                id="tagInput"
   237	                value={tagInput}
   238	                onChange={(e) => setTagInput(e.target.value)}
   239	                className="flex-grow p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-l-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
   240	                placeholder="Add a tag"
   241	                onKeyPress={(e) => {
   242	                  if (e.key === 'Enter') {
   243	                    e.preventDefault();
   244	                    handleAddTag();
   245	                  }
   246	                }}
   247	              />
   248	              <button
   249	                type="button"
   250	                onClick={handleAddTag}
   251	                className="p-2 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded-r-md hover:bg-blue-600"
   252	              >
   253	                Add
   254	              </button>
   255	            </div>
   256	            
   257	            {/* Display tags */}
   258	            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-2">
   259	              {formData.tags.map((tag, index) => (
   260	                <div key={index} className="bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 px-2 py-1 rounded-full flex items-center">
   261	                  <span>{tag}</span>
   262	                  <button
   263	                    type="button"
   264	                    onClick={() => handleRemoveTag(tag)}
   265	                    className="ml-1 text-blue-800 hover:text-blue-900"
   266	                  >
   267	                    &times;
   268	                  </button>
   269	                </div>
   270	              ))}
   271	            </div>
   272	          </div>
   273	          
   274	          {/* Submit buttons */}
   275	          <div className="md:col-span-2 flex justify-end gap-2 mt-4">
   276	            <button
   277	              type="button"
   278	              onClick={onClose}
   279	              className="px-4 py-2 text-gray-700 bg-gray-200 rounded-md hover:bg-gray-300"
   280	            >
   281	              Cancel
   282	            </button>
   283	            <button
   284	              type="submit"
   285	              className="px-4 py-2 text-white bg-blue-500 rounded-md hover:bg-blue-600"
   286	            >
   287	              Add Project
   288	            </button>
   289	          </div>
   290	        </form>
   291	      </div>
   292	    </div>
   293	  );
   294	}
   295	
   296	export default AddProjectOverlay;

File: ./frontend/src/components/auth/Login.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, { useState } from 'react';
     2	import axios from 'axios';
     3	import {API_URL} from '../../constants'
     4	import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
     5	
     6	const LoginForm = () => {
     7	
     8	  const navigate = useNavigate();
     9	  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
    10	  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
    11	
    12	  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
    13	    email: '',
    14	    password: '',
    15	  });
    16	
    17	  const handleChange = (e) => {
    18	    const { name, value } = e.target;
    19	    setFormData((prev) => ({
    20	      ...prev,
    21	      [name]: value,
    22	    }));
    23	  };
    24	
    25	  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    26	    e.preventDefault();    
    27	    console.log('Form submitted:', formData);
    28	    try {
    29	      const response = await axios.post(API_URL + '/auth/login', formData);
    30	      localStorage.setItem('token', response.data.token)
    31	      navigate('/dashboard');
    32	    } catch (error) {
    33	      console.error('Login failed:', error);
    34	      alert('Login failed. Please try again.');
    35	    }
    36	  };
    37	
    38	  return (
    39	    <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen bg-gray-100">
    40	      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="bg-white p-8 rounded-lg shadow-md w-96">
    41	        <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6 text-center">Log In</h2>
    42	        
    43	        <div className="mb-4">
    44	          <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700" htmlFor="email">Email</label>
    45	          <input
    46	            type="email"
    47	            name="email"
    48	            id="email"
    49	            value={formData.email}
    50	            onChange={handleChange}
    51	            required
    52	            className="mt-1 block w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring focus:ring-emerald-500"
    53	            placeholder="Enter your email"
    54	          />
    55	        </div>
    56	
    57	        <div className="mb-4">
    58	          <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700" htmlFor="password">Password</label>
    59	          <input
    60	            type="password"
    61	            name="password"
    62	            id="password"
    63	            value={formData.password}
    64	            onChange={handleChange}
    65	            required
    66	            className="mt-1 block w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring focus:ring-emerald-500"
    67	            placeholder="Enter your password"
    68	          />
    69	        </div>

     1	import React, { useState } from 'react';
     2	import {API_URL} from '../../constants'
     3	import axios from 'axios';
     4	import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
     5	
     6	const Signup = () => {
     7	
     8	  const navigate = useNavigate();
     9	
    10	  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
    11	    name: '',
    12	    email: '',
    13	    phone: '',
    14	    password: '',
    15	    role: 'client', // Default role
    16	  });
    17	
    18	  const handleChange = (e) => {
    19	    const { name, value } = e.target;
    20	    setFormData((prev) => ({
    21	      ...prev,
    22	      [name]: value,
    23	    }));
    24	  };
    25	
    26	  const handleSubmit = async(e) => {
    27	    e.preventDefault();
    28	    try{
    29	    const response = await axios.post(API_URL + '/auth/register', formData);
    30	    navigate('/login');
    31	    }catch (error) {
    32	      console.error(error);
    33	    }
    34	  };
    35	
    36	  return (
    37	    <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen bg-gray-100">
    38	      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="bg-white p-8 rounded-lg shadow-md w-96">
    39	        <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6 text-center">Sign Up</h2>

    45	            name="name"

File: ./frontend/src/components/FileUpload.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, { useState } from 'react';
     2	import { uploadContacts } from '../api';
     3	
     4	const FileUpload = ({ onUpload }) => {
     5	  const [file, setFile] = useState(null);
     6	  const [result, setResult] = useState({ message: '', inserted: 0, skipped: 0 });
     7	
     8	  const handleFileChange = (e) => {
     9	    setFile(e.target.files[0]);
    10	    setResult({ message: '', inserted: 0, skipped: 0 });
    11	  };
    12	
    13	  const handleUpload = async () => {
    14	    if (!file) {
    15	      setResult({ message: 'Please select a file', inserted: 0, skipped: 0 });
    16	      return;
    17	    }
    18	    try {
    19	      const res = await uploadContacts(file);
    20	      setResult({
    21	        message: res.data.message,
    22	        inserted: res.data.inserted,
    23	        skipped: res.data.skipped,
    24	      });
    25	      setFile(null);
    26	      onUpload();
    27	    } catch (err) {
    28	      setResult({ message: err.response?.data?.error || 'Upload failed', inserted: 0, skipped: 0 });
    29	    }
    30	  };
    31	
    32	  return (
    33	    <div>
    34	      <input type="file" accept=".csv" onChange={handleFileChange} />
    35	      <button onClick={handleUpload}>Upload CSV</button>
    36	      {result.message && (
    37	        <p>
    38	          {result.message} (Inserted: {result.inserted}, Skipped: {result.skipped})
    39	        </p>
    40	      )}
    41	    </div>
    42	  );
    43	};
    44	
    45	export default FileUpload;
=================

File: ./frontend/src/components/MessageTable.jsx
----------------
     1	import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
     2	import { API_URL } from '../constants';
     3	import axios from 'axios';
     4	
     5	function MessageTable({ dateRange }) {
     6	  const [messages, setMessages] = useState([]);
     7	  const [mobileId, setMobileId] = useState('');
     8	
     9	  useEffect(() => {
    10	    axios.get(API_URL+'/messages', {
    11	      params: { ...dateRange, mobileId: mobileId || undefined },
    12	    }).then((res) => setMessages(res.data.messages));
    13	  }, [dateRange, mobileId]);
    14	
    15	  return (
    16	    <div>
    17	      <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-4">Message Logs</h2>
    18	      <select
    19	        value={mobileId}
    20	        onChange={(e) => setMobileId(e.target.value)}
    21	        className="mb-4 p-2 border rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
    22	      >
    23	        <option value="">All Phones</option>
    24	        {[...new Set(messages.map(m => m.mobile_id))].map(id => (
    25	          <option key={id} value={id}>{id}</option>
    26	        ))}
    27	      </select>
    28	      <div className="overflow-x-auto">
    29	        <table className="w-full bg-white rounded-lg shadow-md">
    30	          <thead>
    31	            <tr className="bg-gray-200 text-gray-700">
    32	              <th className="p-3 text-left">Contact Name</th>
    33	              <th className="p-3 text-left">Phone Number</th>
    34	              <th className="p-3 text-left">Message</th>
    35	              <th className="p-3 text-left">Status</th>
    36	              <th className="p-3 text-left">Phone ID</th>
    37	              <th className="p-3 text-left">Date</th>
    38	            </tr>
    39	          </thead>
    40	          <tbody>
    41	            {messages.map((msg) => (
    42	              <tr key={msg._id} className="border-t">
    43	                <td className="p-3">{msg.contact_id?.name || 'N/A'}</td>
    44	                <td className="p-3">{msg.contact_id?.phone_number || 'N/A'}</td>
    45	                <td className="p-3">{msg.template_id?.content || 'N/A'}</td>
    46	                <td className="p-3">
    47	                  <span className={`px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-sm ${
    48	                    msg.status === 'Sent' ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700' :
    49	                    msg.status === 'Failed' ? 'bg-red-100 text-red-700' :
    50	                    'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-700'
    51	                  }`}>
    52	                    {msg.status}
    53	                  </span>
    54	                </td>
    55	                <td className="p-3">{msg.mobile_id}</td>
    56	                <td className="p-3">{new Date(msg.datetime).toLocaleString()}</td>
    57	              </tr>
    58	            ))}
    59	          </tbody>
    60	        </table>
    61	      </div>
    62	    </div>
    63	  );
    64	}
    65	
    66	export default MessageTable;

File: ./frontend/src/components/NewLeadForm.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
     2	import axios from 'axios';
     3	import { API_URL } from '../constants';
     4	import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
     5	
     6	const NewLeadForm = () => {
     7	  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
     8	    title: '',
     9	    remark: '',
    10	    client: '',
    11	  });
    12	
    13	  const [managers, setManagers] = useState([]);
    14	  const [clients, setClients] = useState([]);
    15	  const [selectedClientName, setSelectedClientName] = useState(''); // New state for client name
    16	
    17	  const navigate = useNavigate();
    18	
    19	  const handleChange = (e) => {
    20	    const { name, value } = e.target;
    21	
    22	    setFormData((prev) => ({
    23	      ...prev,
    24	      [name]: value,
    25	    }));
    26	
    27	    // If the input is for the client, update the selected client name
    28	    if (name === 'client') {
    29	      const selectedClient = clients.find(client => client._id === value);
    30	      setSelectedClientName(selectedClient ? selectedClient.name : '');
    31	    }
    32	  };
    33	
    34	  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    35	    e.preventDefault();
    36	    try {
    37	      await axios.post(API_URL + '/leads', formData);
    38	      alert('Lead created successfully!');
    39	      navigate('/leads'); // Redirect to leads page or any other page
    40	    } catch (error) {
    41	      console.error(error);
    42	      alert('Error creating lead.');
    43	    }
    44	  };
    45	
    46	  const getManagers = async () => {
    47	    const response = await axios.get(API_URL + '/auth/users/manager');
    48	    setManagers(response.data);
    49	    return response.data;
    50	  };
    51	
    52	  const getClients = async () => {
    53	    const response = await axios.get(API_URL + '/auth/users/client');
    54	    setClients(response.data);
    55	    return response.data;
    56	  };
    57	
    58	  useEffect(() => {
    59	    getManagers();
    60	    getClients();
    61	  }, []);
    62	
    63	  return (
    64	    <div className="bg-white p-8 rounded-lg shadow mt-6 max-w-3xl mx-auto">
    65	      <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold mb-6 text-gray-800">Create New Lead</h2>
    66	      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
    67	        <input
    68	          type="text"
    69	          name="title"
    70	          placeholder="Lead Name"
    71	          value={formData.title}
    72	          onChange={handleChange}
    73	          className="w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-md"
    74	          required
    75	        />
    76	
    77	        <textarea
    78	          name="remark"
    79	          placeholder="Lead Description"
    80	          value={formData.remark}
    81	          onChange={handleChange}
    82	          className="w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-md"
    83	          required
    84	        />
    85	
    86	        <input
    87	          type="text"
    88	          name="requestedData"
    89	          placeholder="Requested Data"
    90	          value={formData.requestedData}
    91	          onChange={handleChange}
    92	          className="w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-md"
    93	        />
    94	
    95	        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
    96	          <input
    97	            type="text"
    98	            list="clients"
    99	            name="client"
   100	            placeholder="Client ID"
   101	            value={selectedClientName} // Display the client name
   102	            onChange={handleChange}
   103	            className="w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-md"
   104	          />
   105	          <datalist id="clients">
   106	            <option value="">Select Client</option>
   107	            {clients.map(client => (
   108	              <option key={client._id} value={client._id}>
   109	                {client.name}
   110	              </option>
   111	            ))}
   112	          </datalist>
   113	        </div>
   114	
   115	        <button
   116	          type="submit"
   117	          className="w-full bg-blue-600 text-white font-semibold py-2 rounded-md hover:bg-blue-700 transition"
   118	        >
   119	          Create Lead
   120	        </button>
   121	      </form>
   122	    </div>
   123	  );
   124	};
   125	
   126	export default NewLeadForm;

File: ./frontend/src/components/NewProjectForm.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
     2	import axios from 'axios';
     3	import {API_URL} from '../constants'
     4	
     5	const NewProjectForm = () => {
     6	  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
     7	    name: '',
     8	    description: '',
     9	    status: 'not_started',
    10	    startDate: '',
    11	    endDate: '',
    12	    progress: 0,
    13	    manager: '',
    14	    teamMembers: '',
    15	    client: '',
    16	    budget: '',
    17	    priority: 'medium',
    18	    customFields: {
    19	      techStack: '',
    20	      location: '',
    21	      deliveryMode: ''
    22	    },
    23	    tags: ''
    24	  });
    25	
    26	  const [managers, setManagers] = useState([]);
    27	  const [clients, setClients] = useState([]);
    28	  const [teamMembers, setTeamMembers] = useState([]);
    29	
    30	  const handleChange = (e) => {
    31	    const { name, value } = e.target;
    32	    if (name.startsWith('customFields.')) {
    33	      const key = name.split('.')[1];
    34	      setFormData((prev) => ({
    35	        ...prev,
    36	        customFields: {
    37	          ...prev.customFields,
    38	          [key]: value
    39	        }
    40	      }));
    41	    } else {
    42	      setFormData((prev) => ({
    43	        ...prev,
    44	        [name]: value
    45	      }));
    46	    }
    47	  };
    48	
    49	  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    50	    e.preventDefault();
    51	    const finalData = {
    52	      ...formData,
    53	      teamMembers: formData.teamMembers.split(',').map(id => id.trim()),
    54	      tags: formData.tags.split(',').map(tag => tag.trim())
    55	    };
    56	
    57	    try {
    58	      await axios.post('/projects', finalData);
    59	      alert('Project created successfully!');
    60	    } catch (error) {
    61	      console.error(error);
    62	      alert('Error creating project.');
    63	    }
    64	  };
    65	
    66	  const getManagers = async ()=>{
    67	    const response = await axios.get(API_URL+'/auth/users/manager');
    68	    setManagers(response.data);
    69	    return response.data;
    70	  }
    71	
    72	  const getClients = async ()=>{
    73	    const response = await axios.get(API_URL+'/auth/users/client');
    74	    setClients(response.data);
    75	    return response.data;
    76	  }
    77	
    78	
    79	  useEffect(() => {
    80	    getManagers()
    81	    getClients()
    82	  }, [])
    83	
    84	  return (
    85	    <div className="bg-white p-8 rounded-lg shadow mt-6 max-w-3xl mx-auto">
    86	      <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold mb-6 text-gray-800">Create New Project</h2>
    87	      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
    88	        <input
    89	          type="text"
    90	          name="name"
    91	          placeholder="Project Name"
    92	          value={formData.name}
    93	          onChange={handleChange}
    94	          className="w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-md"
    95	          required
    96	        />
    97	
    98	        <textarea
    99	          name="description"
   100	          placeholder="Description"
   101	          value={formData.description}
   102	          onChange={handleChange}
   103	          className="w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-md"
   104	          required
   105	        />
   106	
   107	        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
   108	          <select
   109	            name="status"
   110	            value={formData.status}
   111	            onChange={handleChange}
   112	            className="w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-md"
   113	          >
   114	            <option value="not_started">Not Started</option>
   115	            <option value="in_progress">In Progress</option>
   116	            <option value="on_hold">On Hold</option>
   117	            <option value="completed">Completed</option>
   118	            <option value="cancelled">Cancelled</option>
   119	          </select>
   120	
   121	          <select
   122	            name="priority"
   123	            value={formData.priority}
   124	            onChange={handleChange}
   125	            className="w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-md"
   126	          >

   128	            <option value="medium">Medium</option>

   131	          </select>

   138	            className="w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-md"

   140	          />

   174	              </option>

   176	            </select>

   184	            className="w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-md"
   185	          >
   186	            <option value="">Select Client</option>
   187	            {/* Assuming clients is an array of client objects with id and name */}
   188	            {clients.map(client => (
   189	              <option key={client._id} value={client._id}>
   190	                {client.name}
   191	              </option>
   192	            ))}
   193	            </select>
   194	        </div>
   195	
   196	        <input
   197	          type="text"
   198	          name="teamMembers"

   200	          value={formData.teamMembers}
   201	          onChange={handleChange}

   203	        />
   204	        <input

   216	        >
