File: ./frontend/src/components/PhoneStats.jsx
----------------
     1	import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
     2	import axios from 'axios';
     3	import { API_URL } from '../constants';
     4	
     5	function PhoneStats({ dateRange }) {
     6	  const [phoneStats, setPhoneStats] = useState([]);
     7	  const [selectedPhone, setSelectedPhone] = useState(0);
     8	
     9	  useEffect(() => {
    10	    axios.get(API_URL+'/messages/mobile-stats', {
    11	      params: dateRange,
    12	    }).then((res) => setPhoneStats(res.data));
    13	  }, [dateRange]);
    14	
    15	  if (!phoneStats.length) return null;
    16	
    17	  return (
    18	    <div className="mb-8">
    19	      <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-4">Per-Phone Stats</h2>
    20	      <div className="flex gap-2 mb-4 overflow-x-auto">
    21	        {phoneStats.map((phone, index) => (
    22	          <button
    23	            key={phone._id}
    24	            onClick={() => setSelectedPhone(index)}
    25	            className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-md ${selectedPhone === index ? 'bg-blue-500 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200 text-gray-700'} hover:bg-blue-400 hover:text-white`}
    26	          >
    27	            {phone._id}
    28	          </button>
    29	        ))}
    30	      </div>
    31	      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
    32	        <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-lg shadow-md">
    33	          <h3 className="text-lg font-medium text-gray-700">Sent</h3>
    34	          <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-green-600">{phoneStats[selectedPhone].sent}</p>
    35	        </div>
    36	        <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-lg shadow-md">
    37	          <h3 className="text-lg font-medium text-gray-700">Failed</h3>
    38	          <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-red-600">{phoneStats[selectedPhone].failed}</p>
    39	        </div>
    40	        <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-lg shadow-md">
    41	          <h3 className="text-lg font-medium text-gray-700">Pending</h3>
    42	          <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-yellow-600">{phoneStats[selectedPhone].pending}</p>
    43	        </div>
    44	      </div>
    45	    </div>
    46	  );
    47	}
    48	
    49	export default PhoneStats;

File: ./frontend/src/components/SmsDashboard.jsx

     1	import { useState } from 'react';
     2	import StatsOverview from './StatsOverview';
     3	import PhoneStats from './PhoneStats';
     4	import MessageTable from './MessageTable';
     5	
     6	function SmsDashboard() {
     7	  const [dateRange, setDateRange] = useState({
     8	    startDate: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0],
     9	    endDate: new Date(new Date().setDate(new Date().getDate() + 1)).toISOString().split('T')[0],
    10	  });
    11	
    12	  return (
    13	    <div>
    14	      <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-6">SMS Sending Stats</h1>
    15	      <div className="flex gap-4 mb-6">
    16	        <input
    17	          type="date"
    18	          value={dateRange.startDate}
    19	          onChange={(e) => setDateRange({ ...dateRange, startDate: e.target.value })}
    20	          className="p-2 border rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
    21	        />
    22	        <input
    23	          type="date"
    24	          value={dateRange.endDate}
    25	          onChange={(e) => setDateRange({ ...dateRange, endDate: e.target.value })}
    26	          className="p-2 border rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
    27	        />
    28	      </div>
    29	      <StatsOverview dateRange={dateRange} />
    30	      <PhoneStats dateRange={dateRange} />
    31	      <MessageTable dateRange={dateRange} />
    32	    </div>
    33	  );
    34	}
    35	
    36	export default SmsDashboard;

     1	import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
     2	import {API_URL} from '../constants';
     3	import { Pie } from 'react-chartjs-2';
     4	import axios from 'axios';
     5	import { Chart as ChartJS, ArcElement, Tooltip, Legend } from 'chart.js';
     6	
     7	ChartJS.register(ArcElement, Tooltip, Legend);
     8	
     9	function StatsOverview({ dateRange }) {
    10	  const [stats, setStats] = useState({ totalSent: 0, totalFailed: 0, totalPending: 0 });
    11	
    12	  useEffect(() => {
    13	    axios.get(API_URL+'/messages/stats', {
    14	      params: dateRange,
    15	    }).then((res) => setStats(res.data));
    16	  }, [dateRange]);
    17	
    18	  const chartData = {
    19	    labels: ['Sent', 'Failed', 'Pending'],
    20	    datasets: [{
    21	      data: [stats.totalSent, stats.totalFailed, stats.totalPending],
    22	      backgroundColor: ['#10b981', '#ef4444', '#f59e0b'],
    23	    }],
    24	  };
    25	
    26	  return (
    27	    <div className="mb-8">
    28	      <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-4">Aggregated Stats</h2>
    29	      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-3 gap-4 mb-6">
    30	        <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-lg shadow-md">
    31	          <h3 className="text-lg font-medium text-gray-700">Sent</h3>
    32	          <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-green-600">{stats.totalSent}</p>
    33	        </div>
    34	        <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-lg shadow-md">
    35	          <h3 className="text-lg font-medium text-gray-700">Failed</h3>
    36	          <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-red-600">{stats.totalFailed}</p>
    37	        </div>
    38	        <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-lg shadow-md">
    39	          <h3 className="text-lg font-medium text-gray-700">Pending</h3>
    40	          <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-yellow-600">{stats.totalPending}</p>
    41	        </div>
    42	      </div>
    43	      <div className="max-w-md mx-auto">
    44	        <Pie data={chartData} />
    45	      </div>
    46	    </div>
    47	  );
    48	}
    49	
    50	export default StatsOverview;

     1	import React, {useState} from "react";
     2	import axios from 'axios'
     3	
     4	function DeadlineExtension({projectId, onExtensionAdded}) {
     5	    const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
     6	        projectId: projectId,
     7	        newDeadline:"",
     8	        reason:"",
     9	        category:""
    10	    })
    11	
    12	    console.log(projectId)
    13	    const handleSubmit = async(e)=>{
    14	        e.preventDefault()
    15	        const token = localStorage.getItem('token')
    16	        const response =await axios.post(`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/deadline-extensions`,formData, {
    17	            headers:{
    18	                'x-auth-token': token
    19	            }
    20	        })
    21	        console.log(response.data)
    22	        if (onExtensionAdded) {
    23	            onExtensionAdded(response.data);
    24	          }
    25	    }
    26	
    27	    const handleChange = (e)=>{
    28	        const {name, value} = e.target;
    29	        const data = {...formData, [name]:value}
    30	        setFormData(data)
    31	    }
    32	  return (
    33	    <div>
    34	      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="flex justify-between mt-4 p-4 bg-gray-50 border-4 border-green-500 rounded-lg shadow-sm">
    35	        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
    36	          <div className="flex flex-col justify-between">
    37	            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
    38	              New Deadline
    39	            </label>
    40	            <input
    41	              type="date"
    42	              name="newDeadline"
    43	              value={formData.newDeadline}
    44	              onChange={handleChange}
    45	              className="mt-1 p-2 border rounded-md w-full focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-red-300"
    46	              required
    47	            />
    48	          </div>
    49	
    50	          <div className="flex flex-col justify-between">
    51	            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
    52	              Category
    53	            </label>
    54	            <select
    55	              name="category"
    56	              value={formData.category}
    57	              onChange={handleChange}
    58	              className="mt-1 p-2 border rounded-md w-full focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-red-300"
    59	              required
    60	            >
    61	              <option value="">Select category</option>
    62	              <option value="client_delay">client_delay</option>
    63	              {/* <option value="resource">Resource</option>
    64	          <option value="scope">Scope Change</option>
    65	          <option value="other">Other</option> */}
    66	            </select>
    67	          </div>
    68	
    69	          <div className="flex flex-col">
    70	            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
    71	              Reason
    72	            </label>
    73	            <textarea
    74	              name="reason"
    75	              rows="1"
    76	              value={formData.reason}
    77	              onChange={handleChange}
    78	              className="mt-1 p-2 border rounded-md w-full focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-red-300"
    79	              required
    80	            ></textarea>
    81	          </div>
    82	        </div>
    83	
    84	        <div className="mt-4 flex justify-end">
    85	          <button
    86	            type="submit"
    87	            className="px-4 py-2 bg-red-500 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-red-600 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-red-300"
    88	          >
    89	            Add Extension
    90	          </button>
    91	        </div>
    92	      </form>
    93	    </div>
    94	  );
    95	}
    96	
    97	export default DeadlineExtension;

     1	import React, { useState } from "react";
     2	import { useEffect } from "react";
     3	import axios from "axios";
     4	import DeadlineExtension from "../../../components/ui/DeadlineExtension";
     5	
     6	function ProjectDetails({ project }) {
     7	  const [deadlineExtensions, setDeadlineExtensions] = useState([]);
     8	  const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState(
     9	    project ? new Date(project.startDate).toISOString().split("T")[0] : ""
    10	  );
    11	  const [endDate, setEndDate] = useState(
    12	    project ? new Date(project.endDate).toISOString().split("T")[0] : ""
    13	  );
    14	  const handleStartDateChange = (e) => {
    15	    setStartDate(e.target.value);
    16	    // Optionally, notify parent component or update backend here
    17	    // e.g., onUpdateProject({ ...project, startDate: e.target.value });
    18	  };
    19	  const handleEndDateChange = (e) => {
    20	    setEndDate(e.target.value);
    21	    // Optionally, notify parent component or update backend here
    22	    // e.g., onUpdateProject({ ...project, endDate: e.target.value });
    23	  };
    24	
    25	  if (!project) {
    26	    return <p className="p-4 text-gray-600">Select a project from the list.</p>;
    27	  }
    28	
    29	  const fetchExtensions = async () => {
    30	    const token = localStorage.getItem("token");
    31	    try {
    32	      const response = await axios.get(
    33	        `${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/deadline-extensions/${project._id}`,
    34	        {
    35	          headers: {
    36	            "x-auth-token": token,
    37	          },
    38	        }
    39	      );
    40	      setDeadlineExtensions(response.data);
    41	    } catch (error) {
    42	      console.error("Failed to fetch deadline extensions:", error);
    43	    }
    44	  };
    45	  
    46	
    47	  useEffect(() => {
    48	    if (project) {
    49	      fetchExtensions();
    50	    }
    51	  }, [project, endDate]);
    52	
    53	  const handleExtensionAdded = (newExtension) => {
    54	    fetchExtensions();
    55	      setEndDate(newExtension.newDeadline);
    56	  };
    57	
    58	  return (
    59	    <div>
    60	      <div className="">
    61	        <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">{project.name}</h2>
    62	        {project.description && (
    63	          <p className="mb-4 border-b-2 border-blue-300">
    64	            {project.description}
    65	          </p>
    66	        )}
    67	        <div className="flex flex-wrap justify-between items-center gap-2">
    68	          <p>
    69	            <strong>Team Leader:</strong> {project?.team.teamLeader.name}
    70	          </p>
    71	          <div className="flex flex-row gap-2 justify-between items-center">
    72	            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700">
    73	              <strong>Start Date:</strong>
    74	            </label>
    75	            <input
    76	              type="date"
    77	              value={startDate}
    78	              onChange={handleStartDateChange}
    79	              className="mt-1 max-w-60 p-2 text-gray-500 focus:outline-0 focus:shadow-lg"
    80	              disabled
    81	            />
    82	          </div>
    83	          <div className="flex flex-row gap-2 justify-between items-center">
    84	            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700">
    85	              <strong>Start Date:</strong>
    86	            </label>
    87	            <input
    88	              type="date"
    89	              value={endDate}
    90	              onChange={handleEndDateChange}
    91	              className="mt-1 max-w-60 p-2 text-gray-500 focus:outline-0 focus:shadow-lg"
    92	            />
    93	          </div>
    94	          <p>
    95	            <strong>Client:</strong> {project.client.name}
    96	          </p>
    97	          <p>
    98	            <strong>Priority:</strong> {project.priority}
    99	          </p>
   100	          <p className="col-span-2">
   101	            <strong>Tags:</strong>{" "}
   102	            {project.tags ? project.tags.join(", ") : "None"}
   103	          </p>
   104	        </div>
   105	        <div className="mt-4">
   106	          <div className="p-2">
   107	            <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold">Timeline Extensions</h3>
   108	          </div>
   109	
   110	          <div className="overflow-x-auto h-96 shadow-lg">
   111	            <table className="min-w-full bg-white shadow-md rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
   112	              <thead className="bg-red-300 text-white">
   113	                <tr>
   114	                  <th className="text-left p-2 uppercase font-semibold">
   115	                    Updated At
   116	                  </th>
   117	                  <th className="text-left p-2 uppercase font-semibold">
   118	                    New Deadline
   119	                  </th>
   120	                  <th className="text-left p-2 uppercase font-semibold">
   121	                    Reason
   122	                  </th>
   123	                  <th className="text-left p-2 uppercase font-semibold">
   124	                    Category
   125	                  </th>
   126	                </tr>
   127	              </thead>
   128	              <tbody>
   129	                {deadlineExtensions.length > 0 ? (
   130	                  deadlineExtensions.map((extension, index) => (
   131	                    <tr
   132	                      key={index}
   133	                      className="border-b border-gray-200 hover:bg-gray-100"
   134	                    >
   135	                      <td className="p-2">
   136	                        {extension.updatedAt.split("T")[0]}
   137	                      </td>
   138	                      <td className="p-2">
   139	                        {extension.newDeadline.split("T")[0]}
   140	                      </td>
   141	                      <td className="p-2">{extension.reason}</td>
   142	                      <td className="p-2">{extension.category}</td>
   143	                    </tr>
   144	                  ))
   145	                ) : (
   146	                  <tr>
   147	                    <td colSpan="4" className="text-center p-2 text-gray-500">
   148	                      No deadline extensions found.
   149	                    </td>
   150	                  </tr>
   151	                )}
   152	              </tbody>
   153	            </table>
   154	            <DeadlineExtension projectId= {project._id} onExtensionAdded={handleExtensionAdded} />
   155	          </div>
   156	        </div>
   157	      </div>
   158	      {/* Add more project details as needed */}
   159	    </div>
   160	  );
   161	}
   162	
   163	export default ProjectDetails;

     1	import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
     2	import axios from 'axios';
     3	import AddProjectOverlay from '../../../components/AddProjectOverlay';
     4	
     5	function ProjectsList({ projects, onSelectProject, selectedProjectId, onAddProject }) {
     6	  const [isAddOverlayOpen, setIsAddOverlayOpen] = useState(false);
     7	  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState('');
     8	  const [teams, setTeams] = useState([]);
     9	  const [clients, setClients] = useState([]);
    10	  
    11	  // Fetch teams and clients for the dropdown menus
    12	  useEffect(() => {
    13	    // Fetch teams
    14	    const fetchTeams = async () => {
    15	      try {
    16	        const response = await axios.get(`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/teams`);
    17	        if (response.status === 200) {
    18	          setTeams(response.data);
    19	        }
    20	      } catch (error) {
    21	        console.error('Error fetching teams:', error);
    22	      }
    23	    };
    24	
    25	    // Fetch clients
    26	    const fetchClients = async () => {
    27	      try {
    28	        const response = await axios.get(`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/users/clients`);
    29	        if (response.status === 200) {
    30	          setClients(response.data);
    31	        }
    32	      } catch (error) {
    33	        console.error('Error fetching clients:', error);
    34	      }
    35	    };
    36	
    37	    if (isAddOverlayOpen) {
    38	      fetchTeams();
    39	      fetchClients();
    40	    }
    41	  }, [isAddOverlayOpen]);
    42	  
    43	  const filteredProjects = projects?.filter(project => 
    44	    project.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase())
    45	  ) || [];
    46	  
    47	  const handleAddProject = (newProject) => {
    48	    if (onAddProject) {
    49	      onAddProject(newProject);
    50	    }
    51	  };
    52	  
    53	  if (!projects || projects.length === 0) {
    54	    return (
    55	      <div className=''>
    56	        <div className='flex justify-between bg-gray-200 p-2'>
    57	          <div></div>
    58	          <button 
    59	            onClick={() => setIsAddOverlayOpen(true)}
    60	            className='bg-blue-500 pt-1 pb-1 pr-4 pl-4 rounded-md text-white hover:bg-blue-300'
    61	          >
    62	            Add
    63	          </button>
    64	        </div>
    65	        <p className="p-4">No projects found.</p>
    66	        <AddProjectOverlay 
    67	          isOpen={isAddOverlayOpen} 
    68	          onClose={() => setIsAddOverlayOpen(false)} 
    69	          onAddProject={handleAddProject}
    70	          teams={teams}
    71	          clients={clients}
    72	        />
    73	      </div>
    74	    );
    75	  }
    76	
    77	  return (
    78	    <div className=''>
    79	      {/* List header */}
    80	      <div className='flex justify-between bg-gray-200 p-2' >
    81	        <input 
    82	          type="text" 
    83	          placeholder='Search Project' 
    84	          value={searchQuery}
    85	          onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
    86	          className='bg-transparent p-1 rounded-md focus:outline-0 focus:bg-white'
    87	        />
    88	        <button 
    89	          onClick={() => setIsAddOverlayOpen(true)}
    90	          className='bg-blue-500 pt-1 pb-1 pr-4 pl-4 rounded-md text-white hover:bg-blue-300'
    91	        >
    92	          Add
    93	        </button>
    94	      </div>
    95	      <ul>
    96	        {filteredProjects.map(project => (
    97	          <li
    98	            key={project._id}
    99	            className={`p-3 cursor-pointer border-b hover:bg-blue-50 ${selectedProjectId === project._id ? 'bg-blue-100 font-semibold' : ''}`}
   100	            onClick={() => onSelectProject(project._id)}
   101	          >
   102	            {project.name}
   103	          </li>
   104	        ))}
   105	      </ul>
   106	      
   107	      <AddProjectOverlay 
   108	        isOpen={isAddOverlayOpen} 
   109	        onClose={() => setIsAddOverlayOpen(false)} 
   110	        onAddProject={handleAddProject}
   111	        teams={teams}
   112	        clients={clients}
   113	      />
   114	    </div>
   115	  );
   116	}
   117	
   118	export default ProjectsList;

File: ./frontend/src/pages/dashboard/Projects/ProjectsView.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
     2	import ListDetailsPane from '../../../layouts/ListDetailsPane';
     3	import ProjectsList from './ProjectsList';
     4	import ProjectDetails from './ProjectDetails';
     5	import axios from 'axios';
     6	const token = localStorage.getItem('token')
     7	
     8	function ProjectsView() {
     9	  const [projects, setProjects] = useState([]);
    10	  const [selectedProjectId, setSelectedProjectId] = useState(null);
    11	  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    12	  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
    13	
    14	  // Simulate fetching data
    15	  useEffect(() => {
    16	    const fetchProjects = async () => {
    17	      try {
    18	        setLoading(true);
    19	        const response = await axios.get(`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/projects`, {headers:{
    20	            'x-auth-token': token
    21	        }})
    22	        setProjects(response.data);
    23	        // Optionally select the first project by default
    24	        if (response.data.length > 0) {
    25	          setSelectedProjectId(response.data[0]._id);
    26	        }
    27	      } catch (err) {
    28	        console.error("Failed to fetch projects:", err);
    29	        setError(err.message);
    30	      } finally {
    31	        setLoading(false);
    32	      }
    33	    };
    34	
    35	    fetchProjects();
    36	  }, []);
    37	
    38	  const selectedProject = projects.find(p => p._id === selectedProjectId);
    39	
    40	  const handleAddProject = (newProject) => {
    41	    const response = axios.post(`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/projects`, newProject, {headers:{
    42	        'x-auth-token': localStorage.getItem('token')
    43	    }})
    44	    setProjects([...projects, newProject]);
    45	    setSelectedProjectId(newProject._id);
    46	  };
    47	
    48	  if (loading) {
    49	    return <div className="p-4">Loading projects...</div>;
    50	  }
    51	
    52	  if (error) {
    53	    return <div className="p-4 text-red-600">Error: {error}</div>;
    54	  }
    55	
    56	
    57	  return (
    58	    <ListDetailsPane
    59	      leftContent={
    60	        <ProjectsList
    61	          projects={projects}
    62	          onSelectProject={setSelectedProjectId}
    63	          selectedProjectId={selectedProjectId}
    64	          onAddProject={handleAddProject}
    65	        />
    66	      }
    67	      rightContent={
    68	        <ProjectDetails
    69	          project={selectedProject}
    70	        />
    71	      }
    72	    />
    73	  );
    74	}
    75	
    76	export default ProjectsView;

File: ./frontend/src/pages/Leads.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
     2	import Layout from '../components/Layout';
     3	import { Link } from 'react-router-dom';
     4	import { API_URL } from '../constants';
     5	import axios from 'axios';
     6	
     7	const Leads = () => {
     8	  const [leads, setLeads] = useState([]);
     9	  const [selectedLead, setSelectedLead] = useState(null);
    10	  const [isModalOpen, setIsModalOpen] = useState(false);
    11	
    12	  const getLeads = async () => {
    13	    const response = await axios.get(API_URL + '/leads');
    14	    setLeads(response.data);
    15	    return response.data;
    16	  };
    17	
    18	  useEffect(() => {
    19	    getLeads();
    20	  }, []);
    21	
    22	  const statusCounts = (project) => {
    23	    return project.requestedData.reduce((acc, data) => {
    24	      const statusKey = data.isReceived ? 'Y' : 'N';
    25	      if (!acc[statusKey]) {
    26	        acc[statusKey] = 0;
    27	      }
    28	      acc[statusKey]++;
    29	      return acc;
    30	    }, {});
    31	  };
    32	
    33	  const hasPendingRequests = (project) => {
    34	    return project.requestedData.some(data => !data.isReceived);
    35	  };
    36	
    37	  const getStatusColor = (status) => {
    38	    switch (status) {
    39	      case 'In Progress':
    40	        return 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800';
    41	      case 'open':
    42	        return 'bg-green-100 text-green-800';
    43	      case 'At Risk':
    44	        return 'bg-red-100 text-red-800';
    45	      default:
    46	        return 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-800';
    47	    }
    48	  };
    49	
    50	  const handleDelete = async (id) => {
    51	    try {
    52	      const response = await axios.delete(`${API_URL}/api/leads/${id}`);
    53	      if (response.status === 200) {
    54	        setLeads((prevLeads) => prevLeads.filter((lead) => lead._id !== id));
    55	        alert('Lead deleted successfully');
    56	      }
    57	    } catch (error) {
    58	      console.error('Error deleting lead:', error);
    59	    }
    60	  };
    61	
    62	  const handleStatusToggle = async (leadId, dataId, newStatus) => {
    63	    try {
    64	      const response = await axios.patch(`${API_URL}/api/leads/${leadId}/requestedData/${dataId}`, {
    65	        isReceived: newStatus
    66	      });
    67	      if (response.status === 200) {
    68	        setLeads(prevLeads => prevLeads.map(lead => {
    69	          if (lead._id === leadId) {
    70	            return {
    71	              ...lead,
    72	              requestedData: lead.requestedData.map(data => {
    73	                if (data._id === dataId) {
    74	                  return { ...data, isReceived: newStatus };
    75	                }
    76	                return data;
    77	              })
    78	            };
    79	          }
    80	          return lead;
    81	        }));
    82	        // Update selectedLead if it's the one being modified
    83	        if (selectedLead && selectedLead._id === leadId) {
    84	          setSelectedLead({
    85	            ...selectedLead,
    86	            requestedData: selectedLead.requestedData.map(data => {
    87	              if (data._id === dataId) {
    88	                return { ...data, isReceived: newStatus };
    89	              }
    90	              return data;
    91	            })
    92	          });
    93	        }
    94	      }
    95	    } catch (error) {
    96	      console.error('Error updating status:', error);
    97	    }
    98	  };
    99	
   100	  const openModal = (project) => {
   101	    setSelectedLead(project);
   102	    setIsModalOpen(true);
   103	  };
   104	
   105	  const closeModal = () => {
   106	    setSelectedLead(null);
   107	    setIsModalOpen(false);
   108	  };
   109	
   110	  return (
   111	    <Layout>
   112	      <div className="space-y-6">
   113	        <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
   114	          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800">Leads</h1>
   115	          <Link to="/leads/new" className="bg-blue-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-600 transition-colors">
   116	            Create New Lead
   117	          </Link>
   118	        </div>
   119	
   120	        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow overflow-hidden">
   121	          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
   122	            <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
   123	              <thead className="bg-gray-50">
   124	                <tr>
   125	                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
   126	                    Lead Name
   127	                  </th>
   128	                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
   129	                    Status
   130	                  </th>
   131	                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
   132	                    Client
   133	                  </th>
   134	                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
   135	                    Remark
   136	                  </th>
   137	                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
   138	                    Requested
   139	                  </th>
   140	                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
   141	                    Actions
   142	                  </th>
   143	                </tr>
   144	              </thead>
   145	              <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
   146	                {leads.map((project) => (
   147	                  <tr key={project._id} className="hover:bg-gray-50">
   148	                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
   149	                      <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">
   150	                        {project.title}
   151	                      </div>
   152	                    </td>
   153	                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
   154	                      <span
   155	                        className={`px-2 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full ${getStatusColor(
   156	                          project.status
   157	                        )}`}
   158	                      >
   159	                        {project.status}
   160	                      </span>
   161	                    </td>
   162	                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
   163	                      <span className="text-sm text-gray-500">
   164	                        {project.client.name}
   165	                      </span>
   166	                    </td>
   167	                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-500">
   168	                      {project.remark}
   169	                    </td>
   170	                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
   171	                      <button
   172	                        onClick={() => openModal(project)}
   173	                        className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-white ${
   174	                          hasPendingRequests(project) ? 'bg-red-500 hover:bg-red-600' : 'bg-green-500 hover:bg-green-600'
   175	                        }`}
   176	                      >
   177	                        View Requests
   178	                      </button>
   179	                    </td>
   180	                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium">
   181	                      <button className="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-900 mr-3">
   182	                        Edit
   183	                      </button>
   184	                      <button
   185	                        className="text-red-600 hover:text-red-900"
   186	                        onClick={() => handleDelete(project._id)}
   187	                      >
   188	                        Delete
   189	                      </button>
   190	                    </td>
   191	                  </tr>
   192	                ))}
   193	              </tbody>
   194	            </table>
   195	          </div>
   196	        </div>
   197	      </div>
   198	
   199	      {isModalOpen && selectedLead && (
   200	        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-gray-600 bg-opacity-50 overflow-y-auto h-full w-full">
   201	          <div className="relative top-20 mx-auto p-5 border w-96 shadow-lg rounded-md bg-white">
   202	            <div className="mt-3">
   203	              <h3 className="text-lg font-medium text-gray-900 mb-4">{selectedLead.title} - Requested Data</h3>
   204	              <div className="mt-2 space-y-4">
   205	                {selectedLead.requestedData.map((data) => (
   206	                  <div key={data._id} className="flex items-center justify-between border-b pb-2">
   207	                    <div>
   208	                      <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{data.name || 'Data Item'}</p>
   209	                      <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">
   210	                        Status: {data.isReceived ? 'Received' : 'Pending'}
   211	                      </p>
   212	                    </div>
   213	                    <button
   214	                      onClick={() => handleStatusToggle(selectedLead._id, data._id, !data.isReceived)}
   215	                      className={`px-2 py-1 rounded text-white ${
   216	                        data.isReceived ? 'bg-red-500 hover:bg-red-600' : 'bg-green-500 hover:bg-green-600'
   217	                      }`}
   218	                    >
   219	                      Mark as {data.isReceived ? 'Pending' : 'Received'}
   220	                    </button>
   221	                  </div>
   222	                ))}
   223	              </div>
   224	              <div className="mt-4">
   225	                <button
   226	                  onClick={closeModal}
   227	                  className="w-full px-4 py-2 bg-gray-500 text-white rounded hover:bg-gray-600"
   228	                >
   229	                  Close
   230	                </button>
   231	              </div>
   232	            </div>
   233	          </div>
   234	        </div>
   235	      )}
   236	    </Layout>
   237	  );
   238	};
   239	
   240	export default Leads;
